### Post by amosproductions on 2014-10-29
Hi I have mx450  canon printer, the printer is working fine on ubuntu 14.04, however cant get scanner working can anyone advise me am new to linux kevin

---

### Post by Enigma12 on 2014-10-29
Have you downloaded and installed the scanner driver from Canon? It may be available on their website. If not, Google the scanner model +ubuntu or something like that. If it ends in .deb, just double click the file and it should unpack and set itself up.

---

### Post by pdc on 2014-10-30
Hi amosproductions;

Wayne is absolutely right: Canon supply [COLOR="#0000FF"]**ScanGearMP**[/COLOR] to run the scanner on your MX450 series printer/scanner

if you go here [http://support-asia.canon-asia.com/contents/ASIA/EN/0100517701.html?r=s&q=](http://support-asia.canon-asia.com/contents/ASIA/EN/0100517701.html?r=s&q=) and click to download and SAVE the package, you will download scangearmp-mx450series-2.10-1-deb.tar.gz to your [COLOR="#0000FF"]Downloads[/COLOR] folder

__________________

if you open a terminal; (use the Dash search to find it if you do not know how ................)

and copy and paste the commands that are below; into the terminal; using your mouse; and the top line of the terminal; 

after pasting each command; hit the ENTER key .............

[COLOR="#FF0000"]cd Downloads
tar -zxvf scangearmp-mx450series-2.10-1-deb.tar.gz
cd scangearmp-mx450series-2.10-1
./install.sh[/COLOR]

that will start the install script; it will ask you for your sudo password, so have that ready

let us know how it all goes

---
